<time>1509418634657<//time><Rating>5</Rating>< review>
Do not read the negative reviews...

On my vacation, my eye became infected (conjunctivitis) and required immediate attention. I arrived at 7.30am as they opened. The front desk person was extremely courteous and provided all the necessary log in materials.

Immediately following the completion of the forms, I was brought into a treatment room, where a physician's aide took my vitals. She told me the Doctor would be right in. A few minutes later, the Doctor came in and proceeded to examine my eye as well as asking a few questions regarding allergies. She was extremely knowledgeable and explained the course of treatment. I felt I was in good hands.

A prescription was printed and I was on the road to recovery...

I could not have been more comfortable and pleased with the treatment I received. Do not hesitate to use their services... They are terrific.< /review>

<Rating>5<//Rating>< review>
As is the case with much of my travels, I found this place accidentally while randomly exploring the Palisades. I believe I personally enjoy this space because the scenery and views of the coastline and mountains from the Bluffs are insane and almost dramatic, like I'm in a primetime soap opera like Knots Landing and the neighbors meet at The Bluffs for a secret rendezvous or a cliffhanger-style (pun intended) confrontation. It would be cool to be a resident in this neighborhood just for the chances to hang out here on a regular basis.<//review>

< review>
Just alright. Not thing to write home about, and nothing to wanna come back to. The complimentary lunch soup is a hot and sour soup, which reminds you of a chinese restaurant, rather than your typical coconut soup. My husband got the lunch red curry with pork, it comes with rice and salad. The salad has a sweet mayo based dressing, which is typical of your chinese cold appetizer sweet mayo glaze (like the fried sweet mayo prawn dish). Hubby ordered his red curry with Medium spice, and it was good. My pad kee mao (spicy flat rice noodle) with beef was not spicy enough, and i had to request additional chillies to add. My noodle dish came with the same side salad.< /review>

< text>
Black Bear Diner is always a hit and always busy whenever we come.  Today was opening day for Little League 2018 -- so why not?  Honestly, we were in Buttercream's parking lot -- which didn't have a stall to park in ..so we ended up here.
